<review>First time in this store.  I was disappointed with the succulent display inside the store until I realize they have a lot more in the back garden. Personally, I like to get the small ones so I can grow them myself.  I picked up 9 for a total of $40.

The staff at the store are very friendly and helpful.  They checked in with us regularly to see if we need help but they also allow us enough privacy to look around on our own.  One of the succulents I asked for was out of stock, the lady offered to take down my number and call when she has it. This kind of personal service is hard to find nowadays.   I used to go to the one on Bayshore for my succulents and other plants.  This will be my go to place for succulents from now on.</review><gmap_id>0x808f7e5959ad85a7:0x63c4d87dbc4c93bb</gmap_id><Pictures>None</Pictures></record>

So this place isn't that far from me, and I stopped in to see about their plant workshops and to try and learn to take better care of my aloe vera plant. Went there to buy 2 dozen popsicles, two large mangonadas, 2 large drinks and one frescas con crema. Over $70 later, found out that they don't even have a box for the 26 popsicles that I purchased which were melted by the time I came home. Since the plastic covering the ice cream is open at the bottom, when they melted, they spilled all over the plastic bag that she stuffed all of them in. What a waste!

I asked for a cover for the mangonada and I was told that the cup is too large for the cover. Strange, we were just there last weekend and I got a cover for the large then.
